Statistics

#Samples ###one direction t test

x <- c(1,4,3,2,3,4,3,2,3,2,3,4)

#non-directional
t.test(x, mu = 2)
## 
##  One Sample t-test
## 
## data:  x
## t = 3.0794, df = 11, p-value = 0.01048
## alternative hypothesis: true mean is not equal to 2
## 95 percent confidence interval:
##  2.237714 3.428952
## sample estimates:
## mean of x 
##  2.833333

###paired sample t test

x <- c(1,4,3,2,3,4,3,2,3,2,3,4)
y <- c(3,2,5,4,3,2,3,2,1,2,2,3)

#non-directional
t.test(x, y, paired=TRUE)
## 
##  Paired t-test
## 
## data:  x and y
## t = 0.37796, df = 11, p-value = 0.7126
## alternative hypothesis: true difference in means is not equal to 0
## 95 percent confidence interval:
##  -0.8038766  1.1372099
## sample estimates:
## mean of the differences 
##               0.1666667

independent samples t test

x <- c(1,4,3,2,3,4,3,2,3,2,3,4)
y <- c(3,2,5,4,3,2,3,2,1,2,2,3)

#non-directional
my_ttest <- t.test(x, y, var.equal=TRUE)

my_ttest$p.value #using $ sign gets specific values
## [1] 0.6892509
#

fake paired t test

 
a <- replicate(10000,t.test(rnorm(10,0,1),rnorm(10,0,1)))statistic

a
## Error: <text>:2:58: unexpected symbol
## 1:  
## 2: a <- replicate(10000,t.test(rnorm(10,0,1),rnorm(10,0,1)))statistic
##                                                             ^

###printing a clean table

library(broom)

t_results <- t.test(x, y, var.equal=TRUE)
knitr::kable(tidy(t_results))
estimate1 estimate2 statistic p.value parameter conf.low conf.high method alternative
2.833333 2.666667 0.4051902 0.6892509 22 -0.6863784 1.019712 Two Sample t-test two.sided

##ANOVA ### anova template for 2x2

Subjects <- rep(1:10,each=4)
Factor1 <- rep(rep(c("A","B"), each = 2), 10)
Factor2 <- rep(rep(c("1","2"), 2), 10)
DV <- rnorm(40,0,1)

all_data <- data.frame(Subjects = as.factor(Subjects),
                       DV,
                       Factor1,
                       Factor2)

###between-subjects 1 factor template

factor1 <- rep(c("A","B","C"),each = 5) #does each factor 5 times
DV <- rnorm(n=15,mean=0,sd=1)

all_data <- data.frame(DV,factor1)

#run the anova
aov_out <- aov(DV~Factor1, all_data) #dv "~" name of factor
## Error in model.frame.default(formula = DV ~ Factor1, data = all_data, : variable lengths differ (found for 'Factor1')
#all the details of the anova in a summary table
summary(aov_out) 
## Error in summary(aov_out): object 'aov_out' not found

###between-subjects 2 factor template

# run anova
aov_out <- aov(DV~Factor1*Factor2, all_data)
## Error in model.frame.default(formula = DV ~ Factor1 * Factor2, data = all_data, : variable lengths differ (found for 'Factor1')
# summary
summary(aov_out)
## Error in summary(aov_out): object 'aov_out' not found

###repeated-measures 1 factor template - when the subject does each factor

# run anova - error is the name of the variable that we must divide by the factor
aov_out <- aov(DV~Factor1 + Error(Subjects/Factor1), all_data)
## Error in model.frame.default(formula = DV ~ Subjects/Factor1, data = all_data, : variable lengths differ (found for 'Subjects')
# summary
summary(aov_out)
## Error in summary(aov_out): object 'aov_out' not found

###repeated-measures 2 factor

# run anova
aov_out <- aov(DV~Factor1*Factor2 + Error(Subjects/(Factor1*Factor2)), all_data)
## Error in model.frame.default(formula = DV ~ Subjects/(Factor1 * Factor2), : variable lengths differ (found for 'Subjects')
# summary
summary(aov_out)
## Error in summary(aov_out): object 'aov_out' not found
# kable xtable printing
library(xtable)#library "()" means what package
knitr::kable(xtable(summary(aov_out)))#allows me to load a function within a package without loading a package
## Error in summary(aov_out): object 'aov_out' not found
sum_out[[1]]$'F value'
## Error in eval(expr, envir, enclos): object 'sum_out' not found

##Linear Regression

#lm is linear regression
lm(DV~Factor1, all_data)
## Error in model.frame.default(formula = DV ~ Factor1, data = all_data, : variable lengths differ (found for 'Factor1')

#F simulation

A <- c(1,2,3,4)
B <- c(3,4,5,6)
C <- c(5,6,7,8)

conds<- rep(c("A","B","C"), each=4)
DV <- c(A,B,C)
df <- data.frame(conds, DV)
summary (aov(DV~conds,df))
##             Df Sum Sq Mean Sq F value  Pr(>F)   
## conds        2     32  16.000     9.6 0.00586 **
## Residuals    9     15   1.667                   
## ---
## Signif. codes:  0 '***' 0.001 '**' 0.01 '*' 0.05 '.' 0.1 ' ' 1
run_anova <- function(){

A <- rnorm(4,0,1)
B <- rnorm(4,0,1)
C <- rnorm(4,0,1)

conds<- rep(c("A","B","C"), each=4)?
DV <- c(A,B,C)
df <- data.frame(conds, DV)
summary (aov(DV~conds,df))

sum_out <- summary(aov(DV~conds,df))
sum_out[[1]]$`F value`[1]

return(sum_out[[1]]$`F value`[1])
}


save_fs <- replicate(10000,run_anova())
## Warning in if (type == "package") package <- topic: the condition has
## length > 1 and only the first element will be used

## "no documentation of type 'B' and topic 'DV <- c(A, B, C)' (or error in processing help)", "no documentation of type 'B' and topic 'DV <- c(A, B, C)' (or error in processing help)", "no documentation of type 'C' and topic 'DV <- c(A, B, C)' (or error in processing help)", "no documentation of type 'C' and topic 'DV <- c(A, B, C)' (or error in processing help)", "no documentation of type 'C' and topic 'DV <- c(A, B, C)' (or error in processing help)", "no documentation of type 'C' and topic 'DV <- c(A, B, C)' (or error in processing help)"
